		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/draft-viathinksoft-oidip-04.json') !== 'a390f0dd709542c6cf9d986ef7be9c1eb86c82db') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/whois/draft-viathinksoft-oidip-04.json');
		}
	}
}
